{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Mine\+Sweeper\+::\+My\+Form\+::\+My\+Form\+::\+Generate\+Matrix\+Of\+Buttons (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{rows,  }\item[{int}]{cols,  }\item[{int}]{num\+Bombs,  }\item[{array$<$ array$<$ bool $>$\texorpdfstring{$^\wedge$}{\string^} $>$\texorpdfstring{$^\wedge$}{\string^}}]{mine\+Data,  }\item[{array$<$ array$<$ bool $>$\texorpdfstring{$^\wedge$}{\string^} $>$\texorpdfstring{$^\wedge$}{\string^}}]{revealed\+Data,  }\item[{array$<$ array$<$ bool $>$\texorpdfstring{$^\wedge$}{\string^} $>$\texorpdfstring{$^\wedge$}{\string^}}]{flagged\+Data }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [private]}}

generates the grid of buttons with the desired row, col and mine count, or from a file with data for each button initializes a \doxylink{class_mine_field}{Mine\+Field} with the desired row, col and mine count

restarts the game timer

if there is given data (from a text file) it uses it to create the desired buttons

if there is no data given, for where each mine should be, they get placed at random places across the board

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MyForm::InitializeCustomFieldUI()}{MyForm::InitializeCustomFieldUI()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Mine\+Sweeper\+::\+My\+Form\+::\+My\+Form\+::\+Initialize\+Custom\+Field\+UI (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [private]}}

generates the labels and buttons for customizing the game grid below are explained all the parameters for one label only, as for the rest of the labels and buttons in the code the specifics are the same label \"{}rows\+: \"{}

location of the specified object, X and Y coordinates

background color of the object, in a RGB format

setting the font of the object to the custom font

text color of the object, with the default White color from .NET

text in the object

adding the object to the form controls

bringing the object on top of other ones

textbox for input of the row count

label \"{}cols\+: \"{}

textbox for the input of the column count

textbox for the input of the mine (bomb) count

label that stays on top of the \"{}\+NEW GAME\"{} button and activates it upon clicking

Event\+Handler is the link between an event (like a label click in that case) and what happens in the code when that event occurs. In that case, the lbl\+Custom\+Click method is being called

\"{}\+NEW GAME\"{} button, for initializing a grid with the desired from the player specifics

\"{}\+Settings\+: \"{} label

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MyForm::InitializeMenuUI()}{MyForm::InitializeMenuUI()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void Mine\+Sweeper\+::\+My\+Form\+::\+My\+Form\+::\+Initialize\+Menu\+UI (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [private]}}

Initializes the left-\/side menu of the interface, containing \"{}\+Save\"{} game, \"{}\+Load\"{} saved game \"{}\+Exit\"{} the project buttons \"{}\+SAVE\"{} label

button that activates upon clicking the \"{}\+SAVE\"{} label -\/ saves the game state in a .txt file

\"{}\+LOAD\"{} label

button that activates upon clicking the \"{}\+LOAD\"{} label -\/ loads the game state from a .txt file

\"{}\+HINT\"{} label

button that activates upon clicking the \"{}\+HINT\"{} label -\/ clicks on a random non-\/mine button

\"{}\+EXIT\"{} label

button that activates upon clicking the \"{}\+EXIT\"{} label -\/ quits the form

settings pannel

logo

value input pannel -\/ row count

value input pannel -\/ column count

value input pannel -\/ mine count

mine (bomb) image, next to the mine count input pannel

\"{}\+NEW GAME\"{} button image

\"{}\+SAVE\"{} button image

\"{}\+LOAD\"{} button image

\"{}\+HINT\"{} button image

\"{}\+EXIT\"{} button image

sending the images behind the text

creates all the needed components for the project \"{} \texorpdfstring{$^\wedge$}{\string^} \"{} is the .NET equivalent of \"{} \& \"{}

brief description of the objects used\+:

Button\+: a graphical interface element that provides the user a simple way to trigger an event, like clicking or tapping. It often contains text or an icon indicating what will happen when the user interacts with it.

Label\+: a simple control that displays a text string which the user can\textquotesingle{}t modify directly. It\textquotesingle{}s often used to identify other user interface elements or provide short instructions or explanations.

Text\+Box\+: this control allows the user to input text. It\textquotesingle{}s typically used for gathering user input, such as typing in a search query, entering a password, or writing a message.

Picture\+Box\+: a control that displays an image.

Timer\+: a component that allows you to perform an action at specified intervals or to track time passed \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}
